</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A shooting, an act of shooting at someone.</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschuit.html>beschuit</a> (44079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">biscuit</i>, plausibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">bescuit</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twice cooked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Old Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">biscotto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">biscoctum</i>, from Latin <i>(panis) bis coctus</i> "(bread) twice-baked."
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschuit.html>beschuit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschuiten.html>beschuiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschuitje.html>beschuitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>zwieback, <a href = vnd.unilang:rusk.html>rusk</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tweebak</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***beschuldigen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschuldigen.html>beschuldigen</a> (4935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschuldigen.html>beschuldigen</a></i>, replacing older <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beschulden</i> by influence of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schuldich</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuldig.html>schuldig</a></i>). Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schuld.html>schuld</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-igen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschuldigen.html>beschuldigen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to accuse, blame</li></ol>

***beseffen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a> (4712)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*biseffen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bi-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*seffen</i>. The latter part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sabjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to realize</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>Beseffen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not reflexive, but occasionally it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> wrongly used reflexively: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beseffen.html>beseffen</a></i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> probably a contamination of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:realiseren.html>realiseren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to realize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the same meaning, but reflexive.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beslaan.html>beslaan</a> (42551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beslaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslaan.html>beslaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cover, occupy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Noord-Brabant <b><a href = vnd.unilang:beslaat.html>beslaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebied.html>gebied</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 4919 <a href = vnd.unilang:vierkant.html>vierkante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometer.html>kilometer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">North Brabant <b><a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a></b> an area of 4919 square <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometers.html>kilometers</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to surround, <a href = vnd.unilang:envelop.html>envelop</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fog up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ruiten.html>ruiten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:besloegen.html>besloegen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waardoor.html>waardoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>windows</a> <b>fogged up</b> so that I could not see anything anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shoe (a horse with horseshoes)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beslach</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslag.html>beslag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslagen.html>beslagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beslag.html>beslagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> arrest, detention

<li>(metal) cover (e.g. of a book)</li>
<li>a horseshoe</li>
<li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en">batter</span>, a relatively fluid dough <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">more fluid than <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deeg.html>deeg</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>the state of having reached the final decision or having definitively decided upon an arrangement</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beslechten.html>beslechten</a> (55016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beslichten</i>. ***besluipen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:besluipen.html>besluipen</a> (13764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">beslupen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluipen.html>sluipen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besluipen.html>besluipen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sneak up on, stalk, to approach using stealth</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bother constantly, to harass</li></ol>

***besluit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:besluit.html>besluit</a> (2126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besluiten.html>besluiten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besluit.html>besluit</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besluiten.html>besluiten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besluit.html>besluitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>decision (e.g. after consideration of alternatives)</li>
<li>determination (to do or follow through with something)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:besluiteloos.html>besluiteloos</a> (45825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besluit.html>besluit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">decision, conclusion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-less</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>indecisive, not decisive, unable or unwilling to make decisions or reach conlusions</li></ol>

***besnijden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:besnijden.html>besnijden</a> (30702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besniden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijden.html>snijden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:besnijden.html>besnijden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to circumcise

<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bespien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bespien</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">besprēken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bisprekan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bisprekaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spreken.html>spreken</a></i>.
